			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;font-size:4pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:normal">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> &nbsp;R</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">eflects severance and</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> related charges for a headcount reduction to better align with our strategy. Represents a non-GAAP financial measure and reconciliation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> to the most directly compa</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">rable GAAP financial measure is</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> presented in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">schedules accompanying this press release.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:normal;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;font-size:4pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:normal">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> In millions</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> except percentages and per share data or as</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> otherwise noted.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 12pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;font-size:4pt;vertical-align:super;line-height:100%">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> Based </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">on 55.9 m</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">illion</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> weighted-average</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;"> dil</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">uted shares outstanding for FY22 Q1 and 55.8 million </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">weighted-</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">average </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">diluted </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-size:8pt;color:#000000;">shares outstanding for FY21 Q1.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:normal;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 11pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Tahoma;color:#000000;font-size:11pt;background-color: #FFFF00;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:normal;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;vertical-align:baseline;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Erik Gershwind, President and Chief Executive Officer, said, &#x201C;Our fiscal first quarter was a strong start to the year. Av</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">erage daily sales grew 9.9</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">% as we sustained our market share capture rate by outgrowing the Indu</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">strial Production Index by nearly</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> 500 basis points. We translated that top line growth into double digit earnings growth and strong operating expense leverage. Gross margins, on the other hand, came in below our expectations. We implemented countermeasures quickly and saw improvement towards the end of the quarter and into December. We expect gross margins to bounce back in our fiscal second quarter and we </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">expect to achieve</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> our goal of keeping gross margins </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">roughly </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">flat for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">full </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">year.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:normal;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;vertical-align:baseline;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:3pt 0pt 0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:normal;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;vertical-align:baseline;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Kristen Actis-Grande, Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer, added, "We produced double-digit earnings growth in the first quarter due to strong top line performance and excellent cost controls. Adjusted operating expenses as a percentage of sales dropped 70 basis points year over year fueled by productivity improvements. Our Mission Critical initiatives achieved savings of $10 million and we reinvested $7 million in the quarter. Momentum is building in our business and, as of now, we are trending towards the higher end of our annual operating margin framework. We also see low double-digit ADS growth as a possibility for fiscal 2022. If this happens, operating margins would lift beyond the ranges in our annual operating margin framework.&#x201D;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Gershwind concluded, &#x201C;I am encouraged by the recent progress I see in the Company. Looking beyond this fiscal year, we are on track to achieve our goals of growing sales by at least 400 basis points above the Industrial Production Index and returning ROIC to the high-teens by the end of fiscal 2023.&#x201D; </font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;">About MSC </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;">Industrial Supply Co.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font>

		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">MSC Industrial Supply Co. (NYSE:</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">MSM) is a leading North American distributor of metalworking and maintenance, repair and operations (MRO) products and services. We help our customers drive greater productivity, prof</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">itability and growth with approximately</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> &nbsp;2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">.0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> million products, inventory management and other supply chain solutions, and deep expertise from </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">over </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">80 years of working with customers across industries. Our experienced team of more than 6,500 associates is dedicated to working side by side with our customers to help drive results for their businesses - from keeping operations running efficiently today to continuously rethinking, retooling, and optimizing for a more productive tomorrow. For more information on MSC</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;"> Industrial</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;">, please visit mscdirect.com.</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;color:#000000;">Results Excluding Impairment Loss (prior year), Restructuring Costs, Legal Costs, and Other Related Costs and Tax Effects </font></p></td></tr></table></div>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;font-size:9pt;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">To supplement MSC&#x2019;s unaudited selected financial data presented consistent with accounting principles generally accepted in the United States (&#x201C;GAAP&#x201D;), the Company discloses certain non-GAAP financial measures, including non-GAAP gross profit, non-GAAP operating expenses, non-GAAP income from operations, non-GAAP operating margin, non-GAAP provision for income taxes, non-GAAP net income and non-GAAP diluted earnings per share, that exclude impairment loss (prior year), restructuring costs, legal costs for impairment of prepaid PPE during fiscal year 2021, and other related costs and tax effects. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">These non-GAAP financial measures are not presented in accordance with GAAP or an alternative for GAAP financial measures and may be different from similar non-GAAP financial measures used by other companies. The presentation of this additional information is not meant to be considered in isolation or as a substitute for the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures and should only be used to evaluate MSC&#x2019;s results of operations in conjunction with the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:100%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In calculating non-GAAP financial measures, we exclude impairment loss (prior year), restructuring costs, legal costs for impairment of prepaid PPE during fiscal year 2021, and other related costs and tax effects. Management makes these adjustments to facilitate a review of the Company&#x2019;s operating performance on a comparable basis between periods, for comparison with forecasts and strategic plans, for identifying and analyzing trends in the Company&#x2019;s underlying business and for benchmarking performance externally against competitors. We believe that investors benefit from seeing results from the perspective of management in addition to seeing results presented in accordance with GAAP for the same reasons and purposes for which management uses such non-GAAP financial measures.</font>
		</p>
